############################
#
# Expanded Primitive Events
#
############################

namespace = primitivesexpanded

@MTTHCOMMON = 1000
@MTTHMEDIUM = 2500
@MTTHRARE = 4000

##################################
# Vanilla Events
# Reserved 1 - 99
##################################

#Asteroid Lithoids
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.1
	title = primitivesexpanded.1.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.1.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_asteroid_approaching_planet
	show_sound = event_default
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_sapient_planet
			remove_deposit = d_impact_crater
			create_generic_presapient_species = { UPLIFT_TO = LITHOID }
			while = {
				count = 6
				create_pop = { species = last_created_species }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = REMARKABLE
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.1.tooltip
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier2researchreward
			min = @tier2researchmin
			max = @tier2researchmax 
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.1.a
		exclusive_trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_homicidal = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.1.tooltip
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier2researchreward
			min = @tier2researchmin
			max = @tier2researchmax 
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear War - Pre-FTLs regress (Shuttle)
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.2
	title = "observation.207.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = yes
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.207.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = yes
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.207.hive_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = no
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.207.reg_pre_ftl.desc.gestalt
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = no
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.207.hive_pre_ftl.desc.gestalt
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_nuclear_explosion
	show_sound = event_super_explosion
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			nuke_pre_ftls_survivors_effect = yes
		}
		event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
			random_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
				}
				remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
			}
		}
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost = {
			set_event_locked = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = observation.207.a
		custom_tooltip = regress_to_age_tt
		tooltip = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				set_awareness = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear War - Pre-FTLs regress
planet_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.3
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
			}
			observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = primitivesexpanded.4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			nuke_pre_ftls_survivors_effect = yes
			owner = {
				set_awareness = 0
				random_situation = {
					limit = {
						is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
					}
					remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear War - Pre-FTLs regress
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.4
	title = "observation.1406.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = yes
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.1406.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = yes
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.1406.hive_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = no
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.1406.reg_pre_ftl.desc.gestalt
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_regular_empire = no
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = observation.1406.hive_pre_ftl.desc.gestalt
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_nuclear_explosion
	show_sound = event_super_explosion
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
			random_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
				}
				remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = observation.1406.a
		custom_tooltip = regress_to_age_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
				nuke_pre_ftls_survivors_effect = yes
			}
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				set_awareness = 0
				random_situation = {
					limit = {
						is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
					}
					remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Cold War ###
###  5 - 49  ###

# Cold War (Nuclear War)
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.5
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_pre_ftl_age = atomic_age
				has_pre_ftl_age = early_space_age
			}

			capital_scope = {
				is_artificial = no
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
			# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
			random_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
				}
				remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				set_timed_situation_flag = {
					flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
					days = 3600
				}
			}
			#set_country_flag = observation_1400_fired
			remove_country_flag = primitives_politics # current government won't survive the war
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			
			capital_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = { has_country_flag = nukes_disarmed }
					}
					owner = {
						set_country_flag = observation_1400_ended_peacefully
						random_situation = {
							limit = {
								is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
							}
							remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_awareness < 100
							}
							add_awareness = 20
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_awareness >= 60
							}
							add_opinion_modifier = {
								who = root
								modifier = attempted_infiltration
							}
							set_timed_country_flag = {
								flag = nuclear_sabotage_aliens_discovered
								days = 3600
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
						observation_outpost_owner = {
							country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.105 }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { destroy_situation = this }
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							# Planet Depopulated
							planet_event = {
								id = observation.1401 
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.5
								owner = {
									is_militarist = no
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								has_observation_outpost = no
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								owner = {
									has_country_flag = nukes_partially_disarmed
								}
							}
						}
						50 = {
							# Planet Uninhabitable
							planet_event = {
								id = observation.1403
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.5
								owner = {
									is_militarist = no
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.1
								has_observation_outpost = no
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								owner = {
									has_country_flag = nukes_partially_disarmed
								}
							}
						}
						100 = {
							# Pre-FTLs regress to Stone Age
							planet_event = {
								id = observation.1405
							}
						}
						100 = {
							# Pre-FTLs regress several ages
							planet_event = {
								id = primitivesexpanded.3
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		destroy_situation = this
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.6
	title = "primitivesexpanded.6.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.6.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.6.hive_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_settlement
	show_sound = event_planetary_riot
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = WORRYING
			trigger = {
				is_xenophobe = no
				is_homicidal = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.6.a.phobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_xenophobe = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.6.a.tooltip
	}
}

# Cold War Ends
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.7
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_ended_peacefully
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			random_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
				}
				remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.8 }
			}
		}
		destroy_situation = this
	}
}

# owner = pre-FTL country
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.11
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_situation_flag = had_recent_observation_event
			has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_timed_situation_flag = {
			flag = had_recent_observation_event
			days = 1800
		}
		# Event target workaround as 'observation_outpost_owner' is not supported by dynamic scope tags (@ID)
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				save_event_target_as = observing_country
			}
		}
		fire_on_action = {
			on_action = on_monthly_pulse_pre_ftl_cold_war
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear Testing Treaty
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.12
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			current_stage = escalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_test }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_broken }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_missile_crisis }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_test
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.13 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear Proliferation Treaty
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.14
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_test }
		NOR = {
			current_stage = escalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_broken }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_missile_crisis }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.15 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Nuclear Disarmament Treaty
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.16
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build }
		NOR = {
			current_stage = escalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_destroy }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_broken }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_missile_crisis }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_destroy
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.17 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.17
	title = "primitivesexpanded.17.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.17.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.17.hive_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_galactic_senate
	show_sound = event_conversation
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = INTRIGUING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_militarist = yes
					is_pacifist = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.15.pacif.a
			trigger = {
				is_pacifist = yes
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.15.mil.a
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_militarist = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.10.a.tooltip
	}
}

# Broke Nuclear Treaty
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.18
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_test
				has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build
				has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_destroy
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			current_stage = deescalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_broken }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_timed_country_flag = {
				flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_broken
				days = 3600
			}
			switch = {
				trigger = has_country_flag
				observation_1400_no_nuke_destroy = { remove_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_destroy }
				observation_1400_no_nuke_build = { remove_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build }
				observation_1400_no_nuke_test = { remove_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_test }
			}
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.19 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.19
	title = "primitivesexpanded.19.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.19.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				is_hive_mind_pre_ftl = yes
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.19.hive_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_assembly_fight
	show_sound = event_assembly_fight
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = WORRYING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_militarist = yes
					is_pacifist = yes
					is_xenophobe = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.19.pacif.a
			trigger = {
				is_pacifist = yes
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.19.mil.a
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_militarist = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
				is_xenophile = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.19.mil.b
			trigger = {
				is_militarist = yes
				is_xenophile = yes
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.19.phobe.a
			trigger = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.9.a.tooltip
	}
}

# Nuclear Sabotage Discovered
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.20
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { has_country_flag = nukes_disarmed }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = { has_country_flag = nukes_disarmed_weak }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_awareness < 100
				}
				add_awareness = 20
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_awareness >= 60
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					who = root
					modifier = attempted_infiltration
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = nuclear_sabotage_aliens_discovered
					days = 3600
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = nuclear_sabotage_discovered
					days = 1800
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.21 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.21
	title = "primitivesexpanded.21.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				has_awareness < 60
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.21.reg_pre_ftl.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				has_awareness >= 60
			}
		}
		text = primitivesexpanded.21.reg_pre_ftl.high.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_settlement
	show_sound = event_planetary_riot
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = CURSES
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.21.a.tooltip
	}
}

# Cold War Technologies
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.22
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = cold_war_technologies } }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = cold_war_technologies
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.23 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.23
	title = "primitivesexpanded.23.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.23.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_engineering_research
	show_sound = event_laboratory_sound
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = engineering_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = FASCINATING
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.23.a.tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
	}
}

# Peace Protesters
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.26
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			current_stage = escalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_peace_protestors }
			owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = cold_war_still_new } }
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_authoritarian = yes
					is_hive_empire = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_peace_protestors
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.27 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Proxy War
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.28
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			current_stage = deescalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war }
			owner = { has_country_flag = pyrrhic_victory }
			owner = { has_country_flag = decisive_victory }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war # removed after war over
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_first_proxy_war
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.30 days = 360 random = 720 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.29 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.30
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_country_flag = war_escalated
				}
				remove_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated_again
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = decisive_victory
					days = 1800
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					has_country_flag = war_escalated
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					has_country_flag = war_escalated_again
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 4
					has_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again
				}
				remove_country_flag = observation_1400_proxy_war
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated_again
				remove_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = pyrrhic_victory
					days = 3600
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					is_pacifist = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					is_militarist = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = war_escalated }
					}
					set_country_flag = war_escalated
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = war_escalated_again }
					}
					set_country_flag = war_escalated_again
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again }
					}
					set_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = war_escalated_yet_again
					reroll_random = yes
					random_list = {
						4 = { }
						1 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.5
								is_pacifist = yes
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 1.5
								is_militarist = yes
							}
							# Breaks into Nuclear War
							random_situation = {
								limit = { is_situation_type = situation_cold_war }
								situation_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.5 days = 90 random = 90 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.30 days = 360 random = 720 } # repeat
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					exists = observation_outpost_owner
				}
			}
			capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.31 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Missile Crisis
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.32
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			current_stage = deescalation
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_missile_crisis }
			owner = { has_country_flag = observation_1400_no_nuke_build }
			owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = cold_war_still_new } }
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = observation_1400_missile_crisis
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						is_militarist = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						is_pacifist = yes
					}
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						is_militarist = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.25
						is_pacifist = yes
					}
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.36 days = 60 random = 60 }
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.38 days = 60 random = 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.33 }
			}
		}
		set_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
		# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
	}
}

### Dead God ###
### 80 - 99  ###

# Dead God Religion
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.80
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dead_god_planet_hidden
					has_modifier = dead_god_planet
				}
				NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken }
				has_observation_outpost = yes # notification event
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
					observation_outpost_owner = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = dead_god_religion_reveal }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_animism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_monotheism }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				set_country_flag = dead_god_religion_reveal
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.81 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.81
	title = primitivesexpanded.81.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.81.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_unspeakable_horror
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = physics_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = FASCINATING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.mat
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sp
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphile
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_spiritualist = yes }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = physics_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax 
		}
	}
}

# Dead God Psionics
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.82
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = dead_god_psionics }
		NOR = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter
			has_ascension_perk = ap_the_flesh_is_weak
			has_ascension_perk = ap_engineered_evolution
			has_ascension_perk = ap_synthetic_evolution
		}
		NOT = { is_shroudwalker_apprentice_empire = yes }
		NOT = { is_gestalt = yes }
		has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives
		has_country_flag = dead_god_is_real
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				has_modifier = dead_god_planet_hidden
				has_modifier = dead_god_planet
			}
			NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			98 = {
			}
			2 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 4
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				set_country_flag = dead_god_psionics
				set_country_flag = dead_god_advancement # advanced to space age faster
				give_technology = { tech = tech_psionic_theory }
				add_tradition = tr_psionics_adopt
				shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
				owner.capital_scope = {
					save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
				}
				owner = {
					save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								has_observation_outpost = yes
								exists = observation_outpost_owner
							}
						}
					}
					owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.83 days = 5 random = 30 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Dead God Moon Landing
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.86
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = dead_god_moon_landing }
			has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives
			has_country_flag = early_space_age
			capital_scope = {
				has_moon = yes # make sure it hasn't been blown up or something.
				OR = {
					has_modifier = dead_god_planet_hidden
					has_modifier = dead_god_planet
				}
				NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = dead_god_moon_landing
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_country_flag = dead_god_is_real }
					}
					# psionics
					set_country_flag = dead_god_moon_landing_psionic
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = dead_god_psionics
								has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter
								is_shroudwalker_apprentice_empire = yes
							}
							NOR = {
								has_country_flag = dead_god_fully_psionic
								has_tradition = tr_psionics_psionic_assimilation
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.84 days = 30 random = 30 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							NOR = {
								has_country_flag = dead_god_fully_psionic
								has_tradition = tr_psionics_psionic_assimilation
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.82 days = 30 random = 30 }
					}
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = dead_god_is_real
					}
					# materialist
					set_country_flag = dead_god_moon_landing_materialist
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
							shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
						}
						1 = {
						}
					}
					random_owned_pop = { pop_change_ethic = ethic_materialist }
					random_owned_pop = { pop_change_ethic = ethic_materialist }
				}
				2 = {
					# normal
					set_country_flag = dead_god_moon_landing_normal
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.87 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Dead god lashes out psionically at invaders
planet_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.88
	title = "primitivesexpanded.88.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.88.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_unspeakable_horror
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = root

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
		has_ground_combat = no
		is_occupied_flag = no
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_moon = yes # make sure it hasn't been blown up or something.
		OR = {
			has_modifier = dead_god_planet_hidden
			has_modifier = dead_god_planet
		}
		has_planet_flag = dead_god_is_real_planet
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken }
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_angry }
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives }
		}
		any_owned_pop = {
			species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
			OR = {
				is_enslaved = yes
				is_being_purged = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_pop = {
					species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
					NOT = { pop_has_trait = trait_psionic }
				}
			}
			# natives awake psionically
			planet_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.89 days = 30 random = 90 }
		}
		# Dead God awakens
		planet_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.90 days = 180 random = 180 }
		set_planet_flag = dead_god_angry
	}
	
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.88.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_pop = {
					NOT = {
						species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_pop = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
					}
				}
				kill_pop = yes
			}
			random_owned_pop = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
					}
				}
				kill_pop = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			leader = { kill_leader = { show_notification = no } }
		}
	}
}
planet_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.89
	title = "primitivesexpanded.89.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.89.desc"
	picture = "GFX_evt_psionic_battle"
	show_sound = event_mind_over_matter
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			any_owned_pop = {
				species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
				OR = {
					is_enslaved = yes
					is_being_purged = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		owner = {
			every_owned_pop = {
				limit = {
					species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
				}
				modify_species = {
					species = this
					remove_trait = trait_latent_psionic
					add_trait = trait_psionic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.89.a
		owner = {
			every_owned_planet = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_pop = {
						species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = spiritualist_unrest
					days = 7200 # 20 years
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
planet_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.90
	title = "primitivesexpanded.90.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.90.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_unspeakable_horror
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		exists = owner
		any_owned_pop = {
			species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
			OR = {
				is_enslaved = yes
				is_being_purged = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = spiritualist_unrest
		random_owned_pop = {
			limit = {
				species = { has_species_flag = is_worshipper_species }
			}
			save_event_target_as = worshiper_species
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = dead_god_invaders
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.90.a
		set_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country = {
				name = random
				authority = random
				civics = random
				species = event_target:worshiper_species
				ignore_initial_colony_error = yes
				ethos = {
					ethic = "ethic_militarist"
					ethic = "ethic_fanatic_spiritualist"
				}
				flag = random
				type = default
			}
			last_created_country = {
				set_country_flag = dead_god_psionics
				set_country_flag = dead_god_fully_psionic
				set_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives
				add_resource = {
					minerals = 5000
					energy = 5000
					food = 200
					influence = 250
					alloys = 500
				}
				add_500_unity_per_year_passed = yes # scripted effect
				establish_communications_no_message = event_target:dead_god_invaders
				add_opinion_modifier = { 
					who = event_target:dead_god_invaders
					modifier = opinion_insult
				}
				create_fleet = {
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev

						create_ship = {
							name = random
							random_existing_design = science
						}

						set_fleet_stance = evasive				
						set_location = ROOT
						
						owner = {
							create_leader = {
								class = scientist
								sub_type = survey
								name = random
								skill = 4
								species = owner_main_species
							}
						}
						set_leader = last_created_leader
					}			
				}
					
				#constructor
				create_fleet = {
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev
						
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							random_existing_design = constructor
						}
						
						set_fleet_stance = evasive
						set_location = ROOT
					}
				}
				
				#military
				create_fleet = {
					set_take_point = yes
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev
						
						while = {
							count = 6
							create_ship = {
								name = random
								random_existing_design = corvette
							}
						}
						while = {
							count = 2
							create_ship = {
								name = random
								random_existing_design = destroyer
							}
						}
						create_ship = {
							name = random
							random_existing_design = cruiser
						}
						
						set_location = ROOT
						
						owner = {
							create_leader = {
								class = admiral
								species = owner_main_species
								name = random
								skill = 4
							}
						}
						set_leader = last_created_leader
					}
				}
				create_leader = {
					class = scientist
					species = owner_main_species
					name = random
					skill = 3
				}
				create_leader = {
					class = scientist
					species = owner_main_species
					name = random
					skill = 3
				}
				create_leader = {
					class = scientist
					species = owner_main_species
					name = random
					skill = 3
				}
				create_leader = {
					class = governor
					species = owner_main_species
					name = random
					skill = 3
				}
				save_event_target_as = dead_god_country
			}
			solar_system = {
				starbase = {
					set_owner = event_target:dead_god_country
				}
				every_neighbor_system = {
					limit = {
						exists = space_owner
						space_owner = { is_same_value = event_target:dead_god_invaders }
						NOT = {
							any_system_planet  = {
								is_colony = yes
							}
						}
					}
					starbase = {
						set_owner = event_target:dead_god_country
					}
				}
			}
			set_owner = event_target:dead_god_country
			set_capital = yes
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_Death_God"
				settings = {
					can_upgrade = no
					can_disband = no
					can_change_composition = no
					can_change_leader = no
					uses_naval_capacity = no
					spawn_debris = no
					is_boss = yes
				}				
				effect = {					
					set_owner = event_target:dead_god_country
					create_ship = {
						name = "NAME_Camazotz"
						design = "NAME_Shroud_Avatar"
					}
					set_location = root
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
					set_aggro_range = 3000
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = "absorbed_consciousness_2"
						days = -1
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
				}
				event_target:dead_god_country = {
					copy_techs_from = {
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Dead god awakens due to psionic awakening
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.91
	hide_window = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1000
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { is_gestalt = yes }
		has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives
		has_country_flag = dead_god_is_real
		is_playable = yes
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = dead_god_fully_psionic
			has_tradition = tr_psionics_psionic_assimilation
		}
		capital_scope = {
			has_moon = yes # make sure it hasn't been blown up or something.
			OR = {
				has_modifier = dead_god_planet_hidden
				has_modifier = dead_god_planet
			}
			NOT = { has_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken }
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_resource = {
			minerals = 5000
			energy = 5000
			food = 200
			influence = 250
			alloys = 500
			unity = 5000
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_Death_God"
			settings = {
				can_upgrade = no
				can_disband = no
				can_change_composition = no
				can_change_leader = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = yes
			}				
			effect = {				
				set_owner = root
				create_ship = {
					name = "NAME_Camazotz"
					design = "NAME_Shroud_Avatar"
				}
				set_location = root.capital_scope
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
				set_aggro_range = 3000
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = "absorbed_consciousness_2"
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = overlord }
			overlord = {
				ROOT = {
					copy_techs_from = {
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			set_subject_of = { who = none }
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					copy_techs_from = {
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
			set_planet_flag = dead_god_has_awaken
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.92 }
		}
	}
}

		has_planet_flag = dead_god_is_real_planet

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.94
	title = "primitivesexpanded.92.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.94.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_unspeakable_horror
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:shroud_country } }
			create_country = {
				name = "NAME_Creatures_of_the_Shroud"
				type = shroud_spirits
				flag = {
					icon = {
						category = "special"
						file = "the_shroud.dds"
					}
					background= {
						category = "backgrounds"
						file = "00_solid.dds"
					}
					colors={
						"dark_purple"
						"black"
						"null"
						"null"
					}
				}
			}
			last_created_country = {
				establish_communications_no_message = root
				save_global_event_target_as = shroud_country
			}
		}
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_Death_God"
			settings = {
				can_upgrade = no
				can_disband = no
				can_change_composition = no
				can_change_leader = no
				uses_naval_capacity = no
				spawn_debris = no
				is_boss = yes
			}				
			effect = {				
				set_owner = event_target:shroud_country
				create_ship = {
					name = "NAME_Camazotz"
					design = "NAME_Shroud_Avatar"
				}
				set_location = from
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = return_point
				set_aggro_range = 3000
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = "absorbed_consciousness_2"
					days = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.90.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.112
	title = primitivesexpanded.112.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.112.name
	picture = GFX_evt_spy_network
	show_sound = event_espionage_concluded
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from.target = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				from.target = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		locked_random_list = {
			33 = {
				hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = physics_insights }
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier3researchreward
					min = @tier3researchmin
					max = @tier3researchmax
				}
			}
			33 = {
				hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = society_insights }
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = society_research
					value = @tier3researchreward
					min = @tier3researchmin
					max = @tier3researchmax
				}
			}
			33 = {
				hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = engineering_insights }
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = engineering_research
					value = @tier3researchreward
					min = @tier3researchmin
					max = @tier3researchmax
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				from.target = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 10
				OUTPOST = from.target.capital_scope.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		from = {
			spynetwork = {
				add_spy_network_level_on_success_effect = { VALUE = 5 }
			}
			destroy_espionage_operation = this
		}

# Stone Age Metals
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.200
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_primitive = yes
			has_country_flag = stone_age
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_metal_experiments }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_monoliths }
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes # so unobserved primitives don't zip through stone age
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
				observation_outpost_owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_metal_experiments_o } }
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { capital_scope = { has_modifier = mineral_rich } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = { capital_scope = {has_modifier = ultra_rich } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_slow_learners } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_industrious } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_engineers } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_quick_learners } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_intelligent } }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_metal_experiments
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.201 }
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = primitives_metal_experiments_o
					days = 18000
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.201
	title = "primitivesexpanded.201.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.201.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_cavemen
	show_sound = event_pre_ftl_civilization
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = engineering_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = FASCINATING
			trigger = {
				is_xenophile = no
				is_xenophobe = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.201.a.phile
			trigger = {
				is_xenophile = yes
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.201.a.phobe
			trigger = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = primitivesexpanded.201.a.tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 1
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = engineering_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}
	}
}

				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
				observation_outpost_owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_monoliths_o } }
			}
		}

	}
}

situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.204
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_slow_learners } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_industrious } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_engineers } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_quick_learners } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_intelligent } }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_primitive = yes
			has_country_flag = steam_age
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_betharian }

			}

# Enlightenment
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.206
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = renaissance_age
				has_country_flag = steam_age
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_enlightenment }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_enlightenment
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				60 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.207 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# I'm Spartacus
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.208
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_authoritarian = no }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = iron_age
				has_country_flag = late_medieval_age
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_spartacus }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
					AND = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
						observation_outpost_owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_spartacus_o } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_spartacus
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				set_country_flag = primitives_spartacus_o
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.209 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# French Revolution
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.210
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_country_flag = primitives_enlightenment }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_deviants } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_unruly } }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = renaissance_age
				has_country_flag = steam_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_french_revolution }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_decadent }
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
					AND = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
						observation_outpost_owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_french_revolution_o } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_french_revolution
			random_owned_pop = { pop_change_ethic = ethic_egalitarian }
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.212 days = 360 random = 360 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				set_country_flag = primitives_french_revolution_o
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.211 }
			}
		}
		set_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
		# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.211
	title = "primitivesexpanded.211.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.211.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_medieval_alien_civilization
	show_sound = event_public_unrest
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = INTRIGUING
	}
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.211.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				is_democracy = yes
			}
			is_xenophobe = no
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_policy_flag = interference_not_allowed }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 250 }
		}
		observation_breach_effect = {
			RESOLUTION = resolution_pre_ftl_stances_non_interference
		}
		add_resource = {
			energy = -250
			unity = 250
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = { set_country_flag = french_revolution_outside_aid }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.212
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = french_revolution_outside_aid }
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
				}
				owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.214 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
				}
				owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.213 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_situation = {
			limit = {
				is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
			}
			remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.213
	title = "primitivesexpanded.213.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.213.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_open_revolt
	show_sound = event_ground_battle
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = society_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = FASCINATING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					is_civic_shared_burden = yes
					is_democracy = yes
					AND = {
						is_democracy = yes
						is_militarist = yes
					}
					AND = {
						is_autocracy = yes
						is_gestalt = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.213.rev
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_civic_shared_burden = yes
					AND = {
						is_democracy = yes
						is_militarist = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.213.mil_dem
			trigger = {
				is_democracy = yes
				is_militarist = yes
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.213.dem
			trigger = {
				is_democracy = yes
				is_civic_shared_burden = no
				is_militarist = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.213.imp
			trigger = {
				is_autocracy = yes
				is_gestalt = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.213.pacif
			trigger = {
				is_pacifist = yes
				is_democracy = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}

	}
}

# Agrarian Idyll
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.215
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_materialist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				owner_species = {
					OR = {
						is_species_class = PLANT
						is_species_class = FUN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_spiritualist = yes
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe # Isolationists
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				OR = {
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_agrarian }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_conservational }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_plantoid_phototrophic }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_lithoid_empire = no
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = stone_age
				has_country_flag = bronze_age
				has_country_flag = iron_age
				has_country_flag = late_medieval_age
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_agrarian_idyll }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			}
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
			}
			OR = {
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_agrarian }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_sociologists }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_conservational }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_adaptive }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_extremely_adaptive }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_communal }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_plantoid_phototrophic }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_plantoid_radiotrophic }
			}
			NOT = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_wasteful } }
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
					AND = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
						observation_outpost_owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_agrarian_idyll_o } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_agrarian_idyll
			set_country_flag = primitives_politics
			set_pre_ftl_age_effect = { PRE_FTL_AGE = industrial_age }
			increase_pre_ftl_pops_by_age_effect = { PRE_FTL_AGE = industrial_age }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				set_country_flag = primitives_agrarian_idyll_o
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.216 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bronze Age Collapse
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.217
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		situation_progress >= 960
		situation_progress < 1700
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			has_country_flag = bronze_age
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_bronze_age_collapse }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = primitives_bronze_age_collapse }
			current_awareness_level < high
			capital_scope = {
				habitable_structure = no
				is_gaia_world = no
				NOT = { has_modifier = lush_planet }
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = primitives_bronze_age_collapse
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_bronze_age_collapse
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.219 days = 1800 random = 1800 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.218 }
			}
		}
		set_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
		# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.218
	title = "primitivesexpanded.218.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.218.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_alien_hieroglyphics
	show_sound = event_pre_ftl_civilization
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = UNFORTUNATE
			trigger = {
				is_xenophobe = no
				is_homicidal = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = INTRIGUING
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_xenophobe = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.218.b
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_policy_flag = interference_not_allowed }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = food value >= 500 }
		}
		observation_breach_effect = {
			RESOLUTION = resolution_pre_ftl_stances_non_interference
		}
		event_target:pre_ftl_country = { add_awareness = 10 }
		add_resource = {
			food = -500
			unity = 500
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = { set_country_flag = bronze_age_collapse_outside_aid }
		}
	}
}

# Government and Society Events
# Reserved 300 - 499

# owner = pre-FTL country
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.300
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = steam_age
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = machine_age
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = steam_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					NOT = { has_global_flag = primitives_politics_g }
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_situation_flag = had_recent_observation_event
			has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
			owner = { has_country_flag = primitives_politics }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_timed_situation_flag = {
			flag = had_recent_observation_event
			days = 1800
		}
		set_timed_global_flag = { flag = primitives_politics_g days = 18000 }
		owner = { set_country_flag = primitives_politics }
		# Event target workaround as 'observation_outpost_owner' is not supported by dynamic scope tags (@ID)
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				save_event_target_as = observing_country
			}
		}
		fire_on_action = {
			on_action = on_monthly_pulse_pre_ftl_government
		}
	}
}

	}

# Exalted Priesthood
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.302
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = primitives_enlightenment }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_deviants } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_unruly } }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_religious_war }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			}
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_religious_war
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.304 days = 720 random = 720 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.303 }
			}
		}
		set_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
		# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
	}
}

	id = primitivesexpanded.306
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			75 = {
				set_country_flag = primitives_exalted_priesthood
				reroll_random = yes
				random_list = {
					40 = { }
					30 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
					}
					30 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
					}
				}
				shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
					capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.307 }
					}
				}
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						is_pacifist = yes
						is_militarist = yes
					}
				}
				remove_country_flag = primitives_politics # another chance
				random_list = {
					20 = { }
					20 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
					}
					20 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
					}
					40 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
					}
				}
				shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
					capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.308 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_situation = {
			limit = {
				is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
			}
			remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		}
	}
}

# Corporate Dominion
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.309
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_militarist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe }
				has_megacorp = yes
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_corporate_dominion
			change_government = {
				authority = auth_oligarchic
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
				40 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_authoritarian = yes
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_spiritualist = no }
				shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
			}
			else = {
				shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
			}
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.311 days = 7200 random = 7200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.310 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.311
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_situation = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
					has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.311 days = 720 random = 720 } # try again later
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						has_country_flag = corporate_dominion_outside_aid
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						is_egalitarian = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						is_authoritarian = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						is_xenophobe = yes
					}
					remove_country_flag = primitives_corporate_dominion
					reroll_random = yes
					random_list = {
						20 = {
						}
						20 = {
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								is_spiritualist = yes
							}
							shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
							shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
						}
						30 = {
							shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
							shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
						}
						30 = {
							shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
							shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian } }
						shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_megacorp = yes
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
							is_xenophobe = no
						}
						set_country_flag = primitives_shared_burden
						change_government = {
							authority = auth_democratic
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_country_flag = primitives_idealistic_foundation
						change_government = {
							authority = auth_democratic
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							capital_scope = {
								has_observation_outpost = yes
								exists = observation_outpost_owner
							}
						}
						capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
							country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.312 }
						}
