# Shared Burdens
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.313
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_megacorp = yes
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			is_xenophobe = no
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_shared_burden
			change_government = {
				authority = auth_democratic
			}
			random_list = {
				20 = {
				}
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_spiritualist = yes
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_materialist = yes
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
				}
				shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
			}
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.314 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Slave Revolt
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.315
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_deviants } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { owner_species = { has_trait = trait_unruly } }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_decadent }
				has_country_flag = primitives_slavers_guild # potential follow-up event
			}
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = no
				has_country_flag = primitives_slavers_guild
			}
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			remove_country_flag = primitives_slavers_guild
			set_country_flag = primitives_slave_revolt
			change_government = {
				authority = auth_democratic
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
			if = {
				limit = { any_owned_pop = { has_trait = trait_decadent } }
				every_owned_pop = {
					modify_species = {
						species = this
						remove_trait = trait_decadent
					}
					modify_species = {
						species = this
						add_trait = trait_deviants
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.316 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.316

				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.319 days = 7200 random = 7200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

	}

			min = @tier1researchmin

		}

	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.318.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				allows_slavery = no
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
			is_xenophobe = no
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_policy_flag = interference_not_allowed }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= 250 }
		}
		observation_breach_effect = {
			RESOLUTION = resolution_pre_ftl_stances_non_interference
		}
		add_resource = {
			energy = -250
			unity = 250
		}
		if = {

				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }

				VALUE = 10
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = { set_country_flag = slavers_guild_outside_aid }
		}
	}
}

# Mechanists
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.320
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = steam_age
					has_country_flag = machine_age
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				is_authoritarian = no
				is_xenophobe = no
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_decadent }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = trait_slow_learners }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				OR = {
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_industrious }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_intelligent }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_engineers }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_talented }
					owner_species = { has_trait = trait_quick_learners }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_materialist = yes
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			has_origin = origin_default_pre_ftl
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_robot_fascination
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -8 }
			random_list = {
				50 = {
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_industrious }
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_intelligent }
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_engineers }
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_talented }
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_quick_learners }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.322 days = 10800 random = 10800 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.322 days = 14440 random = 14440 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.321 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

	id = primitivesexpanded.324
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = steam_age
							has_country_flag = machine_age
						}
						NOR = {
							owner_species = { has_trait = trait_industrious }
							owner_species = { has_trait = trait_intelligent }
							owner_species = { has_trait = trait_natural_engineers }
							owner_species = { has_trait = trait_talented }
							owner_species = { has_trait = trait_quick_learners }
						}
					}
					any_situation = {
						is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
						has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.324 days = 720 random = 720 } # try again later
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = primitives_mechanist
			set_origin = origin_mechanists
			shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
			set_policy = {
				policy = robot_pop_policy
				option = robot_pops_allowed
				cooldown = yes
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_building = building_primitive_factory
				while = {
					count = 2
					create_pop = {
						species = last_created_species
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
				capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.325 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.325
	title = "primitivesexpanded.325.name"
	desc = primitivesexpanded.325.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_robot_assembly_plant
	show_sound = event_celebration
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = engineering_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = FASCINATING
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = engineering_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}
	}
}

# Democracy falls to dictatorship
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.326
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { is_egalitarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_authoritarian = no
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = steam_age
					has_country_flag = machine_age
				}
			}
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_military_unification
			change_government = {
				authority = auth_dictatorial
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						is_xenophobe = yes
					}
					# Do Nothing
				}
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						is_xenophile = yes
					}
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.328 days = 7200 random = 7200 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.327 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.327
	title = "primitivesexpanded.327.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.327.desc"

				}

				VALUE = 10

		}

				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 10

			authority = auth_democratic

		shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }

				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes

				}
			}
			capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.329 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Global War
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.331
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_warlord }
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_communal }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_weak }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_deviants }
				owner_species = { has_trait = trait_unruly }
			}
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_warlord
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.333 days = 1080 random = 1080 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.332 }
			}
		}
		set_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
		# Setting this flag for the duration of the entire event chain
		# to prevent other observation events from interfering.
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.332
	title = primitivesexpanded.332.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.332.desc

	picture = GFX_evt_victorious_army
	show_sound = event_ground_battle

	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = FASCINATING
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.333
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_pop = {
			kill_pop = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					is_authoritarian = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					is_militarist = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = primitives_military_unification
				change_government = {
					authority = auth_dictatorial
				}
				reroll_random = yes
				random_list = {
					40 = { }
					30 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
					}
					30 = {
						shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -2 }
					}
				}
				shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
				shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				reroll_random = yes
				random_list = {
					75 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							is_xenophobe = yes
						}
						# Do Nothing
					}
					25 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 3
							is_xenophile = yes
						}
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.328 days = 7200 random = 7200 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
					capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.334 }
					}
				}
				random_situation = {
					limit = {
						is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
					}
					remove_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					is_egalitarian = yes
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					is_xenophile = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = global_dictator_defeated
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.338 days = 1080 random = 1080 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							has_observation_outpost = yes
							exists = observation_outpost_owner
						}
					}
					capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.335 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
		if = {
			limit = { any_owned_pop = { has_trait = trait_decadent } }
			every_owned_pop = {
				modify_species = {
					species = this
					remove_trait = trait_decadent
				}
				modify_species = {
					species = this
					add_trait = trait_deviants
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					exists = observation_outpost_owner
				}
			}
			capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.316 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Warrior Culture

	id = primitivesexpanded.340

			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			owner = { is_spiritualist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {

			is_pacifist = no
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes

			random_list = {
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -2 }
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}

				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.341 }

	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.341
	title = "primitivesexpanded.341.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.341.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_victorious_army
	show_sound = event_pre_ftl_civilization
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = society_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = FASCINATING
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 10
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}
	}
}

		}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {

					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.347 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				any_situation = {

				}
			}
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.348 days = 720 random = 720 } # try again later
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NAND = {
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
							OR = {
								has_ethic = ethic_militarist
								has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
							}
						}
					}
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_country_flag = fanatic_purifier_outside_aid
					}
					remove_country_flag = primitives_military_unification
					remove_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier
					set_country_flag = primitives_slave_revolt
					change_government = {
						authority = auth_democratic
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
					random_owned_pop = {
						kill_pop = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							capital_scope = {
								has_observation_outpost = yes
								exists = observation_outpost_owner
							}
						}
						capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
							country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.329 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Imperial Cult
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.349
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion }
			is_spiritualist = yes
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = primitives_imperial_cult
			set_country_flag = cosmic_imperial_cult
			change_government = {
				authority = auth_imperial
			}
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -5 }
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -5 }
			random_list = {
				33 = {
				}
				33 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -5 }
					if = {
						limit = { is_spiritualist = no }
						shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					}
				}
				33 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -5 }
					if = {
						limit = { is_authoritarian = no }
						shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.350 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Death Cult
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.351
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			owner = { has_country_flag = dead_god_original_primitives }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_spiritualist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_pacifist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = { is_egalitarian = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			has_necroids = yes
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion }
				has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_death
			}
			is_materialist = no
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = primitives_death_cult
			random_list = {
				50 = {
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.352 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = primitivesexpanded.352

	desc = primitivesexpanded.352.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_mem_alien_pilgrimage
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:pre_ftl_country
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = society_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = INTRIGUING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.mat
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sp
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphile
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_spiritualist = yes }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax 
			}
		}

					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 10
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax
		}
	}

# Overtuned, Catalytic, or Genetic
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.353
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				is_spiritualist = no
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_xenophobe = no # obsessed with purity
			has_origin = origin_default_pre_ftl
			OR = {
				has_toxoids = yes
				has_plantoids = yes
				has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_country_flag = atomic_age
						has_country_flag = early_space_age
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.355 days = 18000 random = 9000 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.357 days = 7200 random = 7200 }
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = {
				}
				25 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.354 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.357
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_primitive = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_situation = {
					is_situation_type = pre_ftl_tech_progress_situation
					has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.357 days = 357 random = 720 } # try again later
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				3 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_toxoids = no
					}
					set_country_flag = primitives_overtuned
					set_origin = origin_overtuned
					reroll_random = yes
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							every_owned_pop = {
								modify_species = {
									species = this
									add_trait = trait_spliced_adaptability
								}
							}
						}
						1 = {
							every_owned_pop = {
								modify_species = {
									species = this
									add_trait = trait_juiced_power
								}
							}
						}
						1 = {
							every_owned_pop = {
								modify_species = {
									species = this
									add_trait = trait_crafted_smiles
								}
							}
						}
						1 = {
							every_owned_pop = {
								modify_species = {
									species = this
									add_trait = trait_artificial_intelligence
								}
							}
						}
						1 = {
							every_owned_pop = {
								modify_species = {
									species = this
									add_trait = trait_gene_mentorship
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_plantoids = yes }
					}
					set_country_flag = primitives_catalytic
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_plantoids = yes }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						is_plantoid_empire = no
						is_fungoid_empire = no
					}
					set_country_flag = primitives_bloom
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active }
					}
					set_country_flag = primitives_biological_engineering
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
				capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
					country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.358 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Religious Events

# owner = pre-FTL country
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.500
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = {
				is_materialist = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = {
				is_spiritualist = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = renaissance_age
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = steam_age
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = bronze_age
				has_country_flag = iron_age
				has_country_flag = late_medieval_age
				has_country_flag = renaissance_age
				has_country_flag = steam_age
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					NOT = { has_global_flag = mem_primitives_religion_g }
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_situation_flag = had_recent_observation_event
			has_situation_flag = has_ongoing_observation_event_chain
			owner = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_timed_situation_flag = {
			flag = had_recent_observation_event
			days = 1800
		}
		set_timed_global_flag = { flag = mem_primitives_religion_g days = 18000 }
		owner = { set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion }
		# Event target workaround as 'observation_outpost_owner' is not supported by dynamic scope tags (@ID)
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				save_event_target_as = observing_country
			}
		}
		fire_on_action = {
			on_action = on_monthly_pulse_pre_ftl_religion
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner = { remove_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion } # another chance
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = bronze_age }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = cosmic_animism
			random_list = {
				25 = { }
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -1 }
				}
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -1 }
				}
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -1 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.513 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.513
	title = primitivesexpanded.503.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.513.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_mem_alien_pilgrimage
	show_sound = event_pre_ftl_civilization
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = society_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = FASCINATING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.mat
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sp
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphile
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_spiritualist = yes }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax 
		}
	}
}

# Jainism
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.514
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_militarist = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_polytheism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_pantheism }
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = { }
				15 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -1 }
			shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.515 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spiritual Plurality
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.516
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_spiritualist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_materialist = no
			is_xenophobe = no
			is_militarist = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion } # Special Case
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = renaissance_age
				has_country_flag = steam_age
				has_country_flag = industrial_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_plurality
			set_country_flag = cosmic_pantheism
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				33 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				33 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.517 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Atheism
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.518
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_materialist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_spiritualist = no
			# can fire even if another religious event has fired, except if:
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_plurality
				has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_none
				has_country_flag = primitives_imperial_cult
				has_country_flag = primitives_death_cult
				has_country_flag = primitives_exalted_priesthood
				has_country_flag = primitives_feudal_elite
				has_country_flag = primitives_technocracy
				has_country_flag = primitives_mechanist
				has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = industrial_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_none
			set_country_flag = cosmic_atheism
			shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.519 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Titanic Life Worship
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.520
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = renaissance_age }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = steam_age }
			capital_scope = { has_modifier = titanic_life }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = cosmic_animism
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				15 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				15 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.521 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.521
	title = primitivesexpanded.503.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.521.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_mem_alien_pilgrimage
	show_sound = event_pre_ftl_civilization
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = society_insights
			set_predictive_observation_insight = {
				VALUE = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = FASCINATING
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.mat
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sp
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphile
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = mem_primitives.401a.sphobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_spiritualist = yes }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = society_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax 
		}
	}
}

# Secularism
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.522
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_egalitarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_spiritualist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_materialist = no
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = steam_age
				has_country_flag = industrial_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
			# can fire even if another religious event has fired, except if:
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_plurality
				has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_none
				has_country_flag = primitives_imperial_cult
				has_country_flag = primitives_death_cult
				has_country_flag = primitives_exalted_priesthood
				has_country_flag = primitives_feudal_elite
				has_country_flag = primitives_technocracy
				has_country_flag = primitives_mechanist
				has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = cosmic_secularism
			random_list = {
				10 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist 
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				20 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
				40 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian 
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_spiritualist = yes }
				random_list = {
					20 = { 
						shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist 
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
					}
					40 = { 
						shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
					}
					40 = { 
						shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian 
						shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.523 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = primitivesexpanded.523

	desc = primitivesexpanded.523.desc

# Xenophile Religion
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.524
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_xenophobe = no
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
			}
			OR = {
				current_awareness_level = full
				AND = {
					current_awareness_level = high
					pre_ftl_is_observed_with = {
						MISSION = specimen_collection
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.525 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = primitivesexpanded.528
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		}

			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_materialist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes

					has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.519a.sphobe
			trigger = {
				NOR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_materialist = yes }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
					NOT = { current_awareness_level = full }
				}
			}
			add_observation_insight_effect = {
				VALUE = 5
				OUTPOST = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.observation_outpost 
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = physics_research
			value = @tier1researchreward
			min = @tier1researchmin
			max = @tier1researchmax 
		}
	}
}

situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.530
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion_death
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_polytheism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_pantheism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_animism }
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { }
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -1 }
				}
				25 = { 
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -1 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.531 }
			}
		}
	}
}

situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.532
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner = { is_militarist = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_pacifist = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			random_list = {
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_polytheism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_monotheism }
				1 = { set_country_flag = cosmic_animism }
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = 0 }
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.533 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Children of Atom
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.534
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = no
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = stone_age
					has_country_flag = bronze_age
					has_country_flag = iron_age
					has_country_flag = late_medieval_age
					has_country_flag = steam_age
				}
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_materialist = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion } # Special Case
			capital_scope = { is_planet_class = pc_nuked }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = mem_primitives_religion
			set_country_flag = cosmic_animism
			random_list = {
				50 = {
				}
				20 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophobe
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophobe BONUS = -2 }
				}
				30 = {
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
			shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
			shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.535 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Xenophobes blow up observation post
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.700
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 50
			owner = { has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_egalitarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { has_country_flag = atomic_age } # less capable of reaching space
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_destroy_station }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
			has_awareness > 75
			is_xenophobe = yes
			is_pacifist = no
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_timed_country_flag = {
				flag = primitives_destroy_station
				days = 7200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.701 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.701
	title = primitivesexpanded.701.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.701.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_exploding_ship
	show_sound = event_ship_explosion
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			observation_outpost = {
				dismantle = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = TERRIBLE
			trigger = {
				is_xenophobe = no
				is_homicidal = no
				is_pacifist = no
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.701.a.phobe
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					is_xenophobe = yes
					is_homicidal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = primitivesexpanded.701.a.pacif
			trigger = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		tooltip = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
				observation_outpost = {
					dismantle = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# primitives shift to one of our ethics
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.702
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			owner = {
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = machine_age
					has_country_flag = atomic_age
					has_country_flag = early_space_age
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					exists = observation_outpost_owner
					observation_outpost_owner = {
						exists = ruler
						ruler = {
							species = { has_trait = "trait_repugnant" }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					has_observation_outpost = yes
					exists = observation_outpost_owner
					observation_outpost_owner = {
						has_policy_flag = interference_not_allowed
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitive_ethic_shift }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			is_xenophobe = no
			current_awareness_level = full
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitive_ethic_shift
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_xenophile
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_xenophile
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = xenophile BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = authoritarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = egalitarian BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_materialist
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_materialist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = materialist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = spiritualist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_militarist
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_militarist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = militarist BONUS = -2 }
				}
				1 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								observation_outpost_owner = {
									NOR = {
										has_ethic = ethic_pacifist
										has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
									}
								}
							}
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
						}
					}
					shift_ethic = ethic_pacifist
					shift_primitive_pop_ethic = { ETHIC = pacifist BONUS = -2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.703 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# primitives asks for help building FTL
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.704
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { has_country_flag = mem_primitives_moon }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_primitive = yes
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = primitive_ftl_help
				has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier
				has_country_flag = fircon_1495_fired
				#has_country_flag = fircon_2600_fired # can have both if this fired first
			}
			has_country_flag = early_space_age
			current_awareness_level = full
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
				observation_outpost_owner = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = primitive_ftl_help_o
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitive_ftl_help
			#So that you can't have both ship events
			set_country_flag = fircon_1495_fired
			set_country_flag = fircon_2600_fired
		}
		owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
			set_country_flag = primitive_ftl_help_o
			country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.705 }
		}
		set_observation_events_locked = yes
	}
}

ship_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.706
	title = PROJECT_COMPLETE
	desc = primitivesexpanded.706.a.desc
	desc = primitivesexpanded.706.b.desc
	desc = primitivesexpanded.706.c.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_early_space_age
	show_sound = event_airlock
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet.solar_system = {
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = {
					is_star = no
					is_moon = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = lasership_planet_1
			}
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = {
					is_star = no
					is_moon = no
					NOT = {
						is_same_value = event_target:lasership_planet_1
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = lasership_planet_2
			}
		}
		# A space ship appears next to the pre-FTL Space Station
		create_fleet = {
			name = "NAME_Pre_FTL_Laser_Ship"
			effect = {
				set_owner = event_target:pre_ftl_planet.owner
				create_ship = {
					name = "NAME_Pre_FTL_Laser_Ship"
					design = "NAME_Pre_FTL_Laser_Ship"
				}
				set_location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet
				set_fleet_stance = passive
				queue_actions = {
					repeat = {
						find_closest_planet = {
							trigger = {
								id = laser_ship.patrol.1
								is_same_value = event_target:lasership_planet_1
							}
							found_planet = {
								move_to = this
								orbit_planet = this
								wait = {
									duration = 50
								}
							}
						}
						find_closest_planet  = {
							trigger = {
								id = laser_ship.patrol.2
								is_same_value = event_target:lasership_planet_2
							}
							found_planet = {
								move_to = this
								orbit_planet = this
								wait = {
									duration = 50
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		save_event_target_as = observation_post_owner
	}

	option = {
		name = primitivesexpanded.706.a
		owner = {
			add_resource = { minerals = 250 }
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier3unityreward
				min = @tier3unitymin
				max = @tier3unitymax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = engineering_research
				value = @tier3researchreward
				min = @tier2researchmin
				max = @tier2researchmax
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.707 days = 1000 }
					}
					3 = {
						country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.708 days = 1000 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.707
	title = "fircon.1510.name"
	desc = "fircon.1510.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_sabotaged_ship
	show_sound = event_screams
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			owner = { is_primitive = yes } # This is so it can't happen if they are part of your empire now
		}
	}

	immediate = { # The space station and their lasership blows up
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet.owner = {
			every_controlled_ship = {
				fleet = {
					destroy_fleet = this
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "primitivesexpanded.707.a"
		trigger = {
			values_others = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				set_pre_ftl_age_effect = { PRE_FTL_AGE = atomic_age }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = unadavance_tech_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = "primitivesexpanded.707.b"
		trigger = {
			values_others = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = {
				set_pre_ftl_age_effect = { PRE_FTL_AGE = atomic_age }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = unadavance_tech_tt
	}

	after = {
		set_observation_events_unlocked = yes
	}
}

# Spacefaring Commences
country_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.708
	title = "fircon.1515.name"
	desc = "primitivesexpanded.708.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_ship_in_orbit_3
	show_sound = event_ship_thrusters
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			owner = { is_primitive = yes } # This is so it can't happen if they are part of your empire now
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:pre_ftl_planet = {
			solar_system = {
				random_neighbor_system = { save_event_target_as = primitive_ftl_destination }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "fircon.1520.a"
		trigger = {
			values_others = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = fircon.advance_tech
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = { # Flips control of the starbase to the new spacefaring civilization
				achieve_ftl_effect = {
					PRE_FTL = event_target:pre_ftl_country
					OWNER = root
				}
				solar_system = {
					if = {
						limit = { exists = starbase }
						starbase = {
							set_owner = event_target:pre_ftl_country
							if = {
								limit = { has_starbase_size = starbase_outpost }
								set_starbase_size = starbase_starport
								set_starbase_module = {
									slot = 1
									module = shipyard
								}
								set_starbase_module = {
									slot = 2
									module = shipyard
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									NOT = { has_starbase_module = shipyard }
								}
								set_starbase_module = {
									slot = 1
									module = shipyard
								}
								set_starbase_module = {
									slot = 2
									module = shipyard
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						create_starbase = {
							size = starbase_starport
							module = shipyard
							module = shipyard
							owner = event_target:pre_ftl_country
						}
					}
					every_fleet_in_system = {
						limit = {
							owner = { NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:pre_ftl_country } }
							is_mobile = yes
						}
						set_mia = mia_return_home
					}
					add_claims = { 
						who = event_target:system_owner
						num_of_claims = 1
						show_notification = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "fircon.1520.b"
		trigger = {
			values_others = no 
		}
		custom_tooltip = fircon.advance_tech
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pre_ftl_country = { # Retains ownership of starbase as they become spacefaring and instantly colonizes them
				achieve_ftl_effect = {
					PRE_FTL = root
					OWNER = root
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_observation_events_unlocked = yes
	}
}

	id = primitivesexpanded.709

# Primitive Asylum Seekers
situation_event = {
	id = primitivesexpanded.710
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_xenophobe = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			owner = { has_country_flag = primitives_fanatic_purifier }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_egalitarian = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_pacifist = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner = { is_xenophile = yes }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = primitives_asylum }
			is_regular_pre_ftl = yes
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = steam_age
				has_country_flag = industrial_age
				has_country_flag = machine_age
				has_country_flag = atomic_age
				has_country_flag = early_space_age
			}
			current_awareness_level = full
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile }
			capital_scope = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
				exists = observation_outpost_owner
				observation_outpost_owner = {
					OR = {
						is_gestalt = no
						is_servitor_empire = yes
					}
					any_owned_planet = {
						is_under_colonization = no
						is_controlled_by = owner
						has_orbital_bombardment = no
						habitability = { who = root.owner.owner_species value > 0.2 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner.capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_planet
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_ftl_country
			set_country_flag = primitives_asylum
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					capital_scope = {
						has_observation_outpost = yes
						exists = observation_outpost_owner
					}
				}
			}
			owner.capital_scope.observation_outpost_owner = {
				country_event = { id = primitivesexpanded.711 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = primitivesexpanded.711.name
	desc = primitivesexpanded.711.desc
	
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_settlement
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter
	
	location = event_target:pre_ftl_planet

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {

			NOT = { has_policy_flag = interference_not_allowed }
			NOT = { has_policy_flag = refugees_not_allowed }
		}
		observation_breach_effect = {
			RESOLUTION = resolution_pre_ftl_stances_non_interference
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { random_owned_pop = { save_event_target_as = asylum_pop } } }
		random_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				habitability = { who = from.owner_species value > 0.2 }
				is_under_colonization = no
				is_controlled_by = owner

				pop = event_target:asylum_pop
				planet = this
			}
		}
	}

		name = primitivesexpanded.711.b

			random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
		}
